< review>
I'm giving this amazing OTF studio 5 stars only, because Google doesn't allow 10 stars.

I've been a regular client of this studio for quite some time now. I must say that I've been to a numerous OTF studios throughout the country, but this one is undoubtedly a No. 1 studio.

The overall 1-hour plus experience is exemplary. I'm a 5am weekday regular at this studio. The studio Manager and the entire front desk staff, makes sure that the studio is impeccable clean and odor free. The freshness at 5am, while entering the studio is just great way to kick off the workout mood. The front desk staff is THE BEST I've come across in comparison to any OTF studio. Everyone is so cheerful, full of energy and are always on the move, helping all the clients, to make sure that our workout experience is a  complete one.

The Coaches - Quniton, Anthony, Allen, James, Genevieve and Carrie - hands down, are the best in business. The studio & us clients are really lucky & blessed to have these Coaches, with their vast knowledge, they consistently help us challenging to the next level and make sure our form is perfect.
Though its a group personal training class, both of them gives a feel that its a 1 on 1 workout. They understand every client's limitations & potentials.

This studio has 17 stations and the layout is unmatched. The lobby is big and parking is never an issue.

The first class is free; and it doesn't hurt to try it. That's how I started my fitness journey with OTF.
